 epilogue logan i like to clear my head at night , so i usually go for a long walk down by the pier .

 even the most solitary person needs to be reminded that there are other people in the world . 
 that 's just the way life goes . 
 that 's what it means to be a human being . 
 i stared out at the water with a tinge of sadness .

 i watched the waves as they crossed into the rocks , and it seemed to me that waves were like life , they seemed to be so calm , and then out of nowhere , they would come crashing down , bringing destruction in their wake .

 i was still logan martelli , but i was n't the logan martelli .

 people still looked at me in awe and whispered about me , but it was different now . 
 it was different because they were n't whispering about me being a bad boy , they were whispering about my entire life .
